Anecdotes of Wu Zhihui 163

Wei

Central Committee member Wu Zhihui is known to everyone as a pillar of the party and the country who is knowledgeable about the past and the present, and also a famous person who is good at humor. There are many interesting anecdotes about him. Various newspapers have repeatedly described them. I had a cold night talk with a friend who studied in France, involving an anecdote about Wu in France in the past. It seems to be something that Chinese people have not said. I will describe it as follows.

There is a branch of Lyon University in France. It is specially set up for Chinese students who are not at the level to make up for it. Wu once served as the vice president of the branch and brought two of his relatives to study at the school, one male and one female. The female was about 20 years old, and the male was only about 10 years old. The dormitories in the school are separated for men and women and never mixed. However, the male child was too young and relied on the female child to take care of him. The dormitories were isolated and inconvenient. Wu ordered the male relative to live in the female dormitory with the female child. Unexpectedly, within a few days, the students of the whole school were in an uproar, because the female dormitory was not allowed to mix with men, and they reported it to the principal. The principal was originally a stubborn Frenchman, and he thought so. He issued a ban, but it did not involve the surname. The general idea was that men and women are different and should not be mixed. He reiterated the previous ban. The words were quite stern. Wu saw the demonstration and knew that he was mocking himself. He was very angry. He went to the principal's house and questioned him face to face, saying, "You only know men and women, but you don't know the elderly and the young. My relatives are only ten years old. How can they be called adults? How can they have ambiguous behavior?" At that time, the principal was carrying a young daughter in his hand. Wu pointed and laughed and said, "If you are with this daughter, will you also say that it is irregular?" The principal was speechless and apologized with a smile. Wu is not only proficient in French, but also proficient in English. Foreigners admire him very much

Marginal Notes from the Southwest 164

Jie Fei Luge

Dian Xie Yunnan borders the southern wilderness. The mountains and rivers are intertwined and have a high-rise building potential. The climate is like spring all year round. However, it is limited to Kunming and Dali. If you think about Simao Mengzi Mao Nan land, the rainbow plague is very special. Middlemen die every time. Live at home with bright lights at night, saying it makes the gas go away. The oil-stained hat is more dirty and more precious. When gas comes, it covers the nose to avoid being attacked. Therefore, filthy hats are often worth more than gold.

Qian Cheng Guizhou was the last province in China to open customs. The county rule is mostly made during the Republic of China. Before the Republic of China, I heard that the conquerors of the land would let military officers ride horses. From the beginning to the end, the square was wide, so it became the subordinate. Therefore, there are many large landlords in western Guizhou in recent days. The tillers are his soldiers and soldiers. Mr. Xu, a classmate from Sichuan, recently came from Sichuan and said that there was heavy snow along the way east of Kuimen, while the rape blossoms were colored inside Kuimen. Sichuan is blessed by nature, which can be seen here. However, it also leads to misfortune. Sichuan's money and food have recently been paid to the 30th year of the Republic of China, and the seeds of poppy are regarded as the same as the five grains. As a result, the names of taxes are also very numerous. If it is an opium tax, if it is an addict tax, it is a universal and beautiful word. (Unstamped)

Singing and Dancing as Matchmaker 165

Mao Mao

My old friend, Mr. Cai Wenzhun, with his indomitable spirit, and Ms. Wei Yunmei and Ms. Yingbo, jointly founded the Plum Blossom Singing and Dancing Troupe. His contribution is truly remarkable. Recently, he and Ms. Weng Lanhun held an engagement ceremony at the Cai residence in Zhapu, arranged by Ms. Yingbo. On the tenth, they hosted a banquet for relatives and friends at the Yizhixiang Restaurant. Besides the five tigers of the Mei Troupe – Qian Zhongxiu, Zhang Xianlin, Xu Can'ying, Gong Qiuxia, and Zhang Qi – and other troupe members, nearly a hundred guests attended.

A "tall person" played matchmaker, and everyone enjoyed the engaged couple's honey wine. The groom was then asked to report on the engagement process. Mr. Cai spoke eloquently, saying that while the traditional matchmaker is the Old Man Under the Moon, they had a "tall person under the moon." This was because Ms. Yingbo was exceptionally tall, towering over everyone present. He also mentioned that the "tall person under the moon" was the agent of this marriage, while Ms. Xu Can'ying and Ms. Hong Naiqiu were the representatives, acknowledging their significant efforts in bringing it about. Someone in the audience inquired when the "transaction" would be completed, considering the "deal" was finalized today. Mr. Cai blurted out that they would be performing at the Capital Theater in Nanjing starting from the fifteenth, then return to Shanghai to perform "Yang Guifei," and then go to Xiamen. They would be back in Shanghai before the rainy season. Everyone burst into laughter and shouted "rainy season," causing the engaged couple to blush. The power of the maternal uncle! Mr. Cai placed his maternal uncle, the Kunqu opera master Mr. Xu Youfang, in the seat of honor. After Cai's report, the "tall person under the moon" was asked to reenact the proposal. Cai refused. Mr. Youfang then said to me, "Please represent the maternal uncle fully to make it happen." Thus, I, in the capacity of representing the maternal uncle, gave the order. Mr. Cai had no choice but to bow slightly and kiss Ms. Weng's fair hand, whispering, "My dear, do you love me? Will you marry me?" Under the power of the maternal uncle, Ms. Weng had to smile and nod. The guests applauded, and the proposal ceremony was thus completed.

After the meal, they had a photo taken by the New Art Photography Studio to commemorate the occasion. As we were expressing our gratitude to the host, the phonograph in the room began playing "Home, Sweet Home." (Unstamped)

Anecdotes from the Carnival Queen Election 166

Written by Wenchuyi from Manila

In past carnivals, there was an election for a Filipina to be the Carnival Queen. Because the Philippines consists of the three major islands of Luzon, Visayas, and Mindanao, there were also titles for Luzon Queen, Visayas Queen, and Mindanao Queen, representing those with slightly lesser status, appearance, and wealth, similar to having vice-seats beside the main seat. However, this year's event had several particularly interesting aspects that deserve recording.

Changes to the election system. Four or five years ago, the voting rights were held by the shareholders, which made it susceptible to influence from wealth and power. Therefore, an aesthetics committee was specially established. All candidates initially selected by the newspapers had to be judged and evaluated by the committee members. Last year, a certain lady refused to wear a swimsuit, willing to forgo the chance to be selected, and the elected Carnival Queen's Catholic school claimed she was chasing vanity, leading to humiliation (due to wearing a swimsuit for close and distant viewing by the committee members), and expelled her. As a result, the event sparked two different viewpoints and heated debates in society. This year, the system was changed again, with the shareholders conducting the final selection. Ultimately, genuinely beautiful common girls still did not receive public support, and the competition remained among daughters of political figures or wealthy families. The crown-bearer for just over ten days brings great honor to relatives and friends, and also causes a group of lavish young men to fall head over heels.

Worthy of the Dragon Seed. The Filipina selected this year is the daughter of the director of the National Library and a university professor. Her mother was selected as the first Carnival Queen in 1908 and was known as the beauty of the entire island. The selected Luzon Queen is the daughter of a large landowner from Nueva Ecija province. Her cousin was the retiring Carnival Queen of three years prior. Fine daughters blossom within the same family, a rare and delightful occurrence amid the election's clamor.

Unwilling to be a Vice-Queen. On the night of the coronation, the grand ballroom was brightly lit with electric lights, and luxurious carriages competed to wait at the entrance. Carnival officials suddenly received a letter from the Luzon Queen, stating that she had already returned to her hometown to enjoy the pleasures of rural life and was unwilling to live a life of excessive luxury in this vain arena. According to those familiar with the inside story, the Luzon Queen believed her beauty surpassed that of the Filipina Queen and was unwilling to be second to her, thus willing to sacrifice the title. The authorities did not insist on retaining her according to custom and simply filled the position with the candidate who received the next highest number of votes.

May Fourth and Revolution · Fei · Wen · Bao 167

The motivation for Chinese youth to participate in the revolution originated with the May Fourth Movement. The broker No. 54 in the Goods Exchange was an important place where key figures of the Party and the nation gathered. At that time, the arrogance of the warlords was rampant, and men of ambition often hid among the merchants, biding their time. Later, with the establishment of the Whampoa Military Academy, this place became the liaison office in Shanghai. The person in charge was none other than the current Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, Mr. Chen Xizeng. It is worth considering that the number "54" is the product of 6 and 9. In the Book of Changes, 6 is the yin number and 9 is the yang number. With yin and yang complementing each other, Earth and Heaven achieve harmony. If we combine the Arabic numerals 6 and 9, they form the Taijitu symbol. Therefore, the future of political clarity, with virtuous people rising and petty people declining, is rooted in this. (Gratitude)

Travelogue of the South Seas 168

(212) Sacred Flower

Mr. Yang Shuanglin will be going to Siam on the 10th. A friend came from Siam and invited him. I always considered Siam to be the most purely Buddhist country in the world and intended to visit it, but I haven't been able to. Now, I'm in Burma, but Burma is ruled by the British and is not governed by Buddhist principles. Siam, however, is able to govern with pure Buddhism and is fully independent. It has even regained extraterritorial rights, something our country has not been able to do. There must be something special about it. If that's the case, then the notion that Buddhism cannot govern a country is also shattered. My friend said that customs inspections in Siam are very strict for people of any country, not just China. As for the number of Chinese people in Siam, it's hard to say for sure. Some say that the Siamese population is eight or nine million, with Chinese accounting for one-third. However, this is limited by national borders; everyone must be subject to Siamese law, regardless of their ethnicity. To teach in Siam, one must learn the Siamese language. Siamese people revere Buddha and are generous, even showing respect to beggars. My friend believes that the thick customs of Siam and Burma are most likely to avert the disaster of communism in the future. However, they are also affected by economic factors, and their good customs and beautiful habits are unable to resist economic pressure. Material things are not yet developed, hygiene is not emphasized, life is simple, and the view of life is very free. The Siamese royal family, in order to maintain its bloodline, does not intermarry with foreign races, taking their own sisters as queens. This is very different from our country. Siamese Buddha statues differ from those of other countries, with many statues standing in military attire, and few seated statues. They all have their hands in a gesture of resistance. I initially saw this in Penang and didn't find it beautiful. According to people, the reason Siamese Buddha statues are like this is that during a previous robbery by soldiers, the Buddha manifested in this form. Therefore, later, his statue was sculpted like this everywhere. The relationship between China and Siam goes back who knows how long. There's an interesting story: In Mount Jiuhua in Anhui, there was a Buddha statue that achieved enlightenment, who was the brother of the King of Siam, reincarnated as Ksitigarbha. One year, people spread the rumor that the King of Siam's brother was coming to China again. For a time, people welcomed him very enthusiastically. In conclusion, judging from this, there will surely be good relations between China and Siam in the future. Could this be the motivation? Why do our people worship the King of Siam's brother so much? The rumor stems from the saying that the King of Siam's brother is a reincarnation of Ksitigarbha. Mount Jiuhua is Ksitigarbha's pilgrimage site, and women and men come to offer incense every year. Using religious sentiment to connect internationally is also a good diplomatic strategy.

Heartfelt Warmth 169

(3) (7) (1) Bao Tianxiao

Chapter 17: The Art of Preserving Youthful Looks; Cui Dai Mixing with Delicate Eyebrows; No Way to Prolong Life; The Golden Market and Excellent Steed. Yuan Chun carefully looked... at the edge of the watch... a prong holding the diamond had come loose... she used a small pair of tweezers... to put it back in... then took it out again... Tomorrow, she would go to Lao Feng Xiang Silver Store... and ask them to set it properly... The silver store said... we can only set rings and bracelets... we can't handle that kind of watch... you should still go to where you bought it... We can't take on such a solemn task... This remark reminded Hua Lao Liu... that she bought it at Uliwen's... and originally, the foreign company issued a three-year warranty... but now that warranty... has been lost, who knows where... She still remembered that foreigner with the full beard... but now, when she went to Uliwen's... the person serving customers was a Chinese man with a pointed chin... She asked about the foreigner with the full beard... and he said that he went back to his country last winter... She showed him her platinum watch... and said it was bought from your store... The man asked, do you have the warranty? Hua Lao Liu said... I lost it... He asked, when did you buy it, which month and day? She couldn't remember clearly either... The man looked at the watch carefully... and said this is an "imported" item... If the watch's internal mechanism is broken... we have watch repairmen who can fix it for you... But we don't fix the problem of a prong coming loose... because Chinese craftsmen can't do that kind of platinum fine work yet... If it's not important... we can send it to a foreign country for you... Hua Lao Liu heard about sending it to a foreign country and was a little worried... It's just a small prong that came loose... nothing major... She tried using a little rosin and alum to glue it firmly... But because a prong was broken off... it would occasionally snag on her clothes... One night... with one of her two beloved rivals... they were enjoying a sweet dream... she didn't know if Hua Lao Liu's... fortune was bad... or if they were too intimate... and they were hooked together at the neck while sleeping... Hua Lao Liu's wrist... unknowingly rested on the face of the man sleeping next to her... Just as he was about to turn over... he pulled his hand away... The man, in a daze... shouted "Ouch!"... and forcefully pushed Hua Lao Liu away... shouting... what's wrong with you?... Hua Lao Liu, rubbing her sleepy eyes, said... what? Are you sleepwalking?... The man said... look... what is it... that scratched my face?... I'm afraid my face is scratched... Hua Yuan Chun, half-raising herself in bed... turned on a light on top of the mosquito net... and looked carefully... only to see on his cheek near the ear... a broken red mark of more than two inches... not quite three inches long... and said... oh my...

...does it hurt?... The man said... what kind of thing did you bring to bed?... you can also take it off when you sleep... are you afraid someone will steal it?... otherwise... you cherish the thing given to you by your sweetheart... and you refuse to take it off... and other people have to suffer!... Hua Yuan Chun said... alright... I won't wear it, then I won't wear it... don't say more...

Book Review

Outline of Cooperation · Tang Bin 170

Translated by Yin Rangneng

In recent decades, China's economic environment has been influenced by the world, gradually making it appear to be lagging behind. Because financial resources are depleted, various social unrest phenomena often occur. Furthermore, all aspects are affected by economic backwardness. Under these circumstances, we must remedy this economic backwardness crisis with a reasonable method. On the one hand, this means seeking social peace and human happiness. At the same time, we must understand that no one lives in this world without consuming, so we must produce.

There are certainly many ways to produce. We are seeking a reasonable production method that can be realized. What is to be described here is the word "cooperation," which is taken from ordinary dictionaries. Even looking at the definition of the word, it can be understood that it is a kind of interaction between humans, that is, many people combine together and carry out a task according to a common goal. This is certainly a very reasonable economic behavior. In a narrow sense, for example, students in various middle schools and universities in our country mostly have consumer cooperatives, and their achievements are still considerable. However, the meaning of this extends to the same as the cooperation that is to be discussed now, only with differences in scope. Consumer cooperation is a combination of two nouns, so this book "Outline of Cooperation" also discusses the consumer item very clearly.

In our China, any reasonable undertaking often causes people to idealize it into a distorted development. For example, consumer cooperation often tends to be oriented toward a certain class, competing for a limited market. As a result, the cycle of commercial prosperity and decline is inevitably brewed. Saying that this contains a scientific basis, however,

Page 16

such consumer cooperation fundamentally loses its original reasonable true meaning. Regarding this, the section on "Consumers and Society" in this book speaks clearly. Truly, "Cooperation is not a class movement; it is based on the good of all people. It does not recognize classes, nor does it provoke one class against another. It also does not condemn profit-seeking businesses. It sees the value of the methods currently used for trade, calculation, and business management, because these are made from long-term experience, so it goes on to use them to serve consumers." This statement is certainly very correct. The possibility of cooperatives in society can be seen from the fact that in some places, many beneficial services have been completed by cooperation. There are such places in various countries. One in Czechoslovakia can be regarded as a model. There is a village called Briggitch, with 350 households, each of which is a member of the cooperative. Later, most of the village's life depended on this society. This is a place where consumers are organized for the sole purpose of more easily obtaining what they need and protecting their interests in what they enjoy. Regarding its detailed situation and perfect management, the book describes them very thoroughly. From this, we can understand that the organization of consumers for their own benefit has a major relationship with society. Consumers are not a class; they are everyone. What they seek is not the benefit of one class, but the overall happiness of society. Therefore, advocating the cooperative movement is a very meaningful thing.

Because the organization of consumption has lasting possibilities, it is precisely because it is a movement for the happiness of the entire society. One of the purposes of cooperation is also to abolish profiteering and dependence, harmonize capital and labor, and the completion of service and the consumption of things can be harmonized together. The ideal of the "cooperative society" is that artisans are employed by the society and do their best to work and create the best things. And what he manufactures is not sold on the market for profit; they belong to the society he works in, and he is also a member of this society, so all the value he creates, except for the part proposed to do social welfare, and this is also something he has a share in. If this cooperation can be widespread, then society will be secure and also get consolidated defense.

The process of cooperative development is naturally from small to large. There are many large plans that start by running large cooperatives and doing large-scale operations, but they are ineffective. People use some mutual restraints, first unite together, and then learn how to jointly run a small cooperative business. This is how it will be effective. When they have achieved results, they then increase their members. When they are familiar with one type of management, they then promote cooperation in other aspects. Cooperation is an example of evolution in management. In China, the organization of consumer cooperatives in various middle schools and universities is a good phenomenon. It is really worthy of our admiration that students, as intellectuals, can cultivate such a spirit of hard work and service. However, there are still very few such cooperative organizations in society. This is something we should promote as much as possible. I remember that a few years ago, a group of scholars had promoted a cooperative movement, but this wave disappeared and became an illusion in a short period of time.

Under China's economically backward situation, this cooperation for the happiness of all mankind is necessary to pay attention to. However, like a specialized book with correct judgments about the development of this undertaking, it is really rare in our country's current publishing world. Some, mentioning the connection between economy and society, then want to have the purpose of propagating some economic policies of Marxism. This is only another method of disrupting social peace. What is the need for the promotion of a cooperative movement then? Therefore, under this kind of situation, this "Outline of Cooperation" is also worthy of my recommendation. The author, Dr. Hua Baitao, is a well-known authority on American cooperative business. His book can also be seen as a small history of the American cooperative movement. It is very able to find out the true meaning of the cooperative in this, and it can also be used as a reference for other countries preparing to start this business. Here, the author has detailed descriptions of the operation of cooperative methods and the cooperative movement, and has the same attention to the shortcomings and advantages of cooperation. Therefore, what is called cooperation here is discussed from the standpoint of consumers, which is sufficient for general scholars to study. Of course, cooperation is not absolutely the best business method, and it cannot be said that if it is good, people should adopt it. However, it is also very meaningful to express its facts and possibilities and compare it with other methods.

The whole book is divided into eight chapters: (1) Criticism of the Modern Situation, (2) Criticism of the Proposed Relief Methods, (3) The Economics of Cooperation, (4) The Social and Economic Aspects of Cooperation, (5) Methods of Realization, (6) The Shortcomings and Difficulties of Cooperation, (7) The Benefits of Cooperation, (8) All Kinds of People. The descriptions in each chapter have a correct eye and are impartial. This is really the true attitude of research. All matters regarding cooperation are based on the author's knowledge of current cooperative methods, so this book is very worthy of our attention.

Social News

Marshal Foch's Diary of the European War 171

Translated by Gu Angruo

The morality of this idea, and this can be applied to commanders at all levels, is that the more uneasy the state of his troops and the more critical the situation in front of him, the more urgently any commander should use his indomitable courage to fulfill his part of the responsibility in the overall war situation. He must never let himself be affected by the uncertainty and danger of his part, because the success of the overall situation can often restore them to their original state. Conversely, it is his responsibility to anxiously and exhaustively devise ways to support his troops through critical periods. My opinion is that the victory of Marne has completely proven this statement to be true. Now is the time to apply it again.

On October 8, after General Franché, the commander of the front lines, established his command headquarters in Albévy, he came to see me in Toulon. This was the first time I had encountered him since the start of the war. It was very pleasant to meet an old friend. We knew each other well. He treated me very well when he was previously in France and England. Our relationship could always be open and honest. Now, we were once again in the same boat in the great war.

One of the pieces of news he brought was about the surrender of Antwerp. He asked me what methods we could use to overthrow the Germans, who had already taken control of Belgium. I replied that we still had no contact with the Belgian army, and our troops were still far from the north coast. In my opinion, the question was whether we could achieve these two goals in time. Now, if we cannot outflank the enemy's northern flank, we should use all our strength to do so.

My old friend Sir Henry Wilson (who later became the commander of the front lines) was with Sir John Franché. I told him I was happy to see him again, and I told him that I firmly believed that the prompt and powerful addition of the British army to the battle group was entirely the result of his proper arrangement as chief of staff. General Wilson had long shown his patriotic vigilance and far-sighted vision, and later operational experience further proved this.

Personally, I didn't think the general war situation was so bad, and I was very confident. I had seen the enemy's defeat in Rouen, and we had repelled them in Marne. The enemy now very much wanted to regain their situation in the north, but we could also maintain our position. Their plan to quickly and overwhelmingly defeat the French army in one battle had failed. The strength of the Russian army would soon be deployed, and the battle achievements of our Second and Tenth Armies and the participation of the British army proved that our northward strategy was very promising. Therefore, on October 10, I wrote to the commander-in-chief saying,

General, I think our situation is very satisfactory. Costerneau is not moving, and Mar is attacking Arras. His success is very slow, but he is still advancing. Further north, our cavalry has just retreated back to the Bussy-Boisnes line, but I don't think there is any relationship, because the British Second Corps will arrive in Boisnes and Lilles at noon today, and the British cavalry regiment will also arrive in Aire and Garbecque. Furthermore, British troops are arriving in Saint-Omer (our defense zone) and its suburbs today to disembark. Under these circumstances, there is no need to fear the German attack. (To be continued)
